INC-SOURCE (REAC) Neutron beam passed through a filter made of    3181600100024 
             Pb (9 cm), boron carbide (1 cm) and Cd (1 mm) - NRI  3181600100025

INC-SPECT  The fission fast neutron spectrum (En>1.5 MeV) can be  3181600100028 
            approximated by exp(-0.75 En) law.                    3181600100029 
           The reactor neutron spectrum (En>1.0 MeV) can be       3181600100030 
            approximated by exp(-0.7 En) law.                     3181600100031 
COMMENT    By Lee Bernstein (2019-12-15):                         3181600100032 
            We found that a Maxwellian with kT~1.4 MeV is optimum 3181600100033 
            to reproduce the 56Fe(n,n'gamma) intensities in the   3181600100034 
            atlas from the TOF measurement with the GAINS         3181600100035 
            detector array at GELINA reported in Negret et al.    3181600100036 
            Phys.Rev.C90(2014)034602 (EXFOR 23703).               3181600100037 
DETECTOR   (GELI) Shielded by Fe (5 cm), paraffin with boron      3181600100038
